***дослать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дослать.html>досла́ть</a> (5617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дослать.html>досла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doslátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">досыла́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send the remainder <i>(of)</i>, to send on, to send in addition
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дослать.html>досла́л</a></b> 200 <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>doslál</b> 200 rubléj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he sent on (another) two hundred roubles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seat, to chamber</li></ol>

***дослушать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дослушать.html>дослу́шать</a> (13186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дослушать.html>дослу́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doslúšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дослу́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to listen to the whole/rest <i>(of)</i>, to hear through/out, to sit out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дослушать.html>дослу́шать</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:половина.html>полови́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>doslúšatʹ</b> štó-libo do polovíny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to listen to the first half of smth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дослушать.html>дослу́шал</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on menjá ne <b>doslúšal</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he didn't wait until I finished; he interrupted me halfway (through my story)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досмотреть.html>досмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dosmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досматривать.html>досма́тривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dosmátrivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досмотреть.html>досмотре́ть</a></b>)

***доставать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a> (2858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reach, to touch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потоло́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зкий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достаю́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Potolók takój nízkij, što ja do nevó <b>dostajú</b> rukój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The ceiling is so low that I (can) reach it with my hand.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take, to go fetch, to take out</li>
<li>to get, to procure, to obtain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy someone badly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffice</li></ol>

<li>раздобывать, заполучать, <a href = vnd.unilang:приобретать.html>приобрета́ть</a></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доставаться.html>достава́ться</a> (8193)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставаться.html>достава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достаться.html>доста́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall to one's share; to fall to one's lot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Им <b><a href = vnd.unilang:достаться.html>доста́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тре</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Im <b>dostálisʹ</b> lúčšije mestá v teátre.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">They got the best seats in the theater.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>Ей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:достаться.html>доста́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нелегкий.html>нелёгкая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́ля</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jej <b>dostálasʹ</b> neljóxkaja dólja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">An uneasy fate fell to her lot.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доставаться.html>достаю́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty dáže ne znáješʹ, kak <b>dostajútsja</b> éti dénʹgi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You don't even know how this money is gained.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***доставить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доставить.html>доста́вить</a> (2349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставить.html>доста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставлять.html>доставля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deliver, to convey, to supply, to furnish</li>
<li>to procure, to cause, to give</li>
<li>to give, to provide, to afford</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доставка.html>доста́вка</a> (10415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставить.html>доста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доставлять.html>доставля́ть</a> (5123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставить.html>доста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставлять.html>доставля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставить.html>доста́вить</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:достаток.html>доста́ток</a> (11846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достаток.html>доста́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostátok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достаток.html>доста́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достаток.html>доста́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достаток.html>доста́тков</a></b>)

<ol><li>prosperity, (good) fortune; sufficiency</li>
<li>welfare</li></ol>

***достать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́ть</a> (746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reach, to touch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ленького</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рост.html>ро́ста</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полок.html>по́лки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On málenʹkovo rósta, ne <b>dostánet</b> do vérxnej pólki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is of short stature and won't reach the top shelf.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take, to go fetch, to take out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигарета.html>сигаре́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закурить.html>закури́л</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>dostál</b> iz karmána sigaréty i zakuríl.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He took some cigarettes out of his pocket and started smoking.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get, to procure, to obtain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>Где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a>?</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to a female</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Gde ty <b>dostála</b> étu knígu?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Where did you get (obtain) this book from?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy someone badly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:достать.html>доста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сами</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On menjá <b>dostál</b> so svoími voprósami.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He's a real pest with his questions.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffice</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достигать.html>достига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достигаться.html>достига́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostigátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дости́чься</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дости́гнуться</b>)
